        <script>
            function resetDistrictSelection() {
                return true;
            }

            function openCityModal() {
                var modal = document.getElementById('cityModal');
                modal.classList.add('open');
                document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
                setTimeout(function(){
                    document.getElementById('modalCitySearch').focus();
                }, 100);
            }
            
            function closeCityModal() {
                var modal = document.getElementById('cityModal');
                modal.classList.remove('open');
                document.body.style.overflow = '';
            }
            
            document.getElementById('cityModal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (e.target === this) {
                    closeCityModal();
                }
            });

            document.addEventListener('keydown', function(event) {
                if (event.key === "Escape") {
                    closeCityModal();
                }
            });

            function filterModalCities() {
                var input = document.getElementById("modalCitySearch");
                var filter = input.value.toLocaleUpperCase('tr-TR');
                var grid = document.getElementById("modalCityGrid");
                var cards = grid.getElementsByClassName("city-card");
                var emptyState = document.getElementById("emptyState");
                var visibleCount = 0;

                for (var i = 0; i < cards.length; i++) {
                    var span = cards[i].getElementsByClassName("city-name")[0];
                    if (span) {
                        var textValue = span.textContent || span.innerText;
                        if (textValue.toLocaleUpperCase('tr-TR').indexOf(filter) > -1) {
                            cards[i].style.display = "";
                            visibleCount++;
                        } else {
                            cards[i].style.display = "none";
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                if(visibleCount === 0) {
                    emptyState.style.display = 'block';
                } else {
                    emptyState.style.display = 'none';
                }
            }
        </script>

<script>
    var catSearchTimer;
    var baseUrl = "https://benimisyerim.net/";

    function openCategoryModal() {
        var modal = document.getElementById('categoryModal');
        modal.classList.add('open');
        document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        
        var cards = document.querySelectorAll('.cat-card');
        cards.forEach((card, index) => {
            card.style.opacity = '0';
            card.style.transform = 'translateY(20px)';
            setTimeout(() => {
                card.style.transition = 'all 0.4s ease';
                card.style.opacity = '1';
                card.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
            }, 50 + (index * 10)); 
        });

        setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('catSearchInput').focus(), 150);
    }

    function closeCategoryModal() {
        var modal = document.getElementById('categoryModal');
        modal.classList.remove('open');
        document.body.style.overflow = '';
        setTimeout(() => {
            document.getElementById('catSearchInput').value = '';
            // Modali kapatinca listeyi resetle (AJAX ile ilk 20yi getir)
            filterCategories();
        }, 300);
    }
    
    document.getElementById('categoryModal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (e.target === this) closeCategoryModal();
    });
    
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'Escape') closeCategoryModal();
    });
    
    function filterCategories() {
        var term = document.getElementById('catSearchInput').value;
        var grid = document.getElementById('categoryGrid');
        
        clearTimeout(catSearchTimer);
        
        catSearchTimer = setTimeout(function() {
            var formData = new FormData();
            formData.append('term', term);
            
            // Loading efekti (opaklik düşür)
            grid.style.opacity = '0.7';
            
            fetch(baseUrl + 'ajax-kategori-ara', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            })
            .then(response => response.text())
            .then(html => {
                grid.innerHTML = html;
                grid.style.opacity = '1';
                
                // Yeni gelen elemanlara animasyon
                var cards = grid.querySelectorAll('.cat-card');
                cards.forEach((card, index) => {
                    // Sadece ilk kez görünüyorsa animasyon verilebilir ama hepsi yeni
                    card.style.animation = 'fadeInUp 0.3s ease forwards';
                    card.style.animationDelay = (index * 0.03) + 's';
                    card.style.opacity = '0'; 
                });
            })
            .catch(error => {
                console.error('Kategori Arama Hatasi:', error);
                grid.style.opacity = '1';
            });
        }, 300); // 300ms bekleme (yazarken sürekli istek gitmesin)
    }
</script>

<style>
@keyframes fadeInUp {
    from {
        opacity: 0;
        transform: translateY(20px);
    }
    to {
        opacity: 1;
        transform: translateY(0);
    }
}
</style>

<style>
    .password-toggle-wrapper {
        position: relative;
        display: block;
    }
    .password-toggle-wrapper > input {
        padding-right: 44px !important;
    }
    .password-toggle-btn {
        position: absolute;
        right: 12px;
        top: 50%;
        transform: translateY(-50%);
        border: 0;
        background: transparent;
        color: #8a8a8a;
        cursor: pointer;
        padding: 2px;
        line-height: 1;
        font-size: 16px;
    }
    .password-toggle-btn:hover {
        color: #4a4a4a;
    }
</style>

<script>
    (function () {
        function initPasswordToggles() {
            var inputs = document.querySelectorAll(
                '#girisform form.register input[type="password"], ' +
                '#sign-in-dialog form.register input[type="password"], ' +
                'form input[name="kullanici_sifre"][type="password"]'
            );

            inputs.forEach(function (input) {
                if (input.dataset.eyeInit === "1") {
                    return;
                }
                input.dataset.eyeInit = "1";

                var wrapper = document.createElement("span");
                wrapper.className = "password-toggle-wrapper";

                input.parentNode.insertBefore(wrapper, input);
                wrapper.appendChild(input);

                var btn = document.createElement("button");
                btn.type = "button";
                btn.className = "password-toggle-btn";
                btn.setAttribute("aria-label", "Şifreyi göster");
                btn.setAttribute("aria-pressed", "false");
                btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-regular fa-eye" aria-hidden="true"></i>';

                btn.addEventListener("click", function () {
                    var icon = btn.querySelector("i");
                    var isHidden = input.type === "password";

                    input.type = isHidden ? "text" : "password";
                    btn.setAttribute("aria-pressed", isHidden ? "true" : "false");
                    btn.setAttribute("aria-label", isHidden ? "Şifreyi gizle" : "Şifreyi göster");

                    if (icon) {
                        icon.classList.toggle("fa-eye", !isHidden);
                        icon.classList.toggle("fa-eye-slash", isHidden);
                    }
                });

                wrapper.appendChild(btn);
            });
        }

        if (document.readyState === "loading") {
            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", initPasswordToggles);
        } else {
            initPasswordToggles();
        }
    })();
</script>
